ESFM v0.5 GEN

Note: This is still a very early look into the unfinished text of the Open English Translation of the Bible. Please double-check the text in advance before using in public. Some things (like capitalisation of “him” referring to Jesus or “father” referring to God) in the RV haven’t been decided yet so we’re still testing both ways.

Note: The Readers’ Version on the left is a translation into contemporary English aimed at the person on the street who hasn’t necessarily been brought up with exposure to Biblical jargon and/or 16th century English. It’s designed to be used alongside the Literal Version on the right which gives the English reader a window into what’s actually written in the original languages. (See the introduction for more details—we recommend that you read the introduction first if you’re wanting to fully understand the Literal Version.) By comparing the left and right columns, you should be able to easily get the message of the text, while at the same time keeping an eye on what it was actually translated from.

Genesis

It is our prayer that the Open English Translation of the Bible will give you clear understanding of the accounts and messages written by the God-inspired Biblical writers.

Introduction

The kaluwasan te lalag Hinisis, “bunsuranan”. This baseen, here nasulat ka peggimu te langit and te tane, ka migpuunan te person, and ka bunsuranan te sale and peg-antus here te world. Nasulat again here ka story concerning the keet-etawan in-alam te God and ka peg-uyan din kandan diye te inged promised din kandan.

Nabaad te daruwa this se baseen:

1.) The peggimu te world and ka story concerning the people. Kayi egkabasa ka story concerning ki Adan and ki Iba, ka concerning ki Kain and ki Abil, and ka concerning ki Noah and ka pegsipuk te weyig, and ka concerning the matikang house diye te Babil.

2.) The story concerning the first elders te Israilita. Si Abraham ka first elder te Israilita neyimu mabantug tenged te pegpalintutuu and pegsalig din and te pegtuman din te suhu te God. Egpakasinundul also ka story concerning the anak din si Isaac, and ka apu din si Jacob (egngaranan ded also ki Israel), and ka sapulu and daruwa (12) anak of Jacob iyan migpuunan te sapulu and daruwa (12) descendants te Israel. Nahuhud also here ka concerning the anak of Jacob si Husi and ka neyitabu kandin iyan impuunan te nekeendiye te Egypt si Jacob duma te me anak din.

Egkabasa ta again here ka story concerning the nalein-lein people nabuhal-buhal here te ampew te tane and migmannenasud e. Labew te langun, nahuhud here ka dakel himu te God peggimu te langit and tane and te langun nakatahu here.

Diye te katamanan te story, egkahuhud ka ware egtamanan saad te God te keet-etawan din. Kene eglingawan te God ka saad din and kene din iya egbalaharen ka keet-etawan din su egpanuluen and egbulihan din sikandan. Ne sikandin ka eggukum and eglegpad te langun eggimu te mareet.

Main components of this “book”

The peggimu te God te langit and te world 1:1-2:25

The bunsuranan te sale and te peg-antus 3:1-24

The story ki Adan peendiye te ki Noah 4:1-5:32

Si Noah and ka pegsipuk te weyig 6:1-10:32

The matikang house diye te Babil 11:1-9

The story ki Sim peendiye te ki Abraham 11:10-32

The elders te me Hebrews: si Abraham, si Isaac, and si Jacob 12:1-35:29

The descendants of Isaw 36:1-43

Si Husi and ka me suled din 37:1-45:28

The me Hebrews diye te Egypt 46:1-50:26

See also the FAQs and the Glossary.
